#### `BOQWizardState`

- **Import**: `import { BOQWizardState } from "@/components/boq/BOQProcessingWizard";`
- **Kind**: Type

**Definition**:

```ts
export interface BOQWizardState {
  // Step 1: Upload
  file: File | null;
  uploadId: string | null;
  metadata: {
    sourceDescription: string;
    contractorName: string;
    projectId: string;
    province: string;
    buildingType: string;
    tenderDate: Date | undefined;
  };
  
  // Step 2: Sheets
  parsedSheets: ParsedSheet[];
  selectedSheets: Set<string>;
  
  // Step 3: Columns
  columnMappings: Record<string, ColumnMapping>;
  
  // Step 4: Match (after AI processing)
  matchingStatus: 'idle' | 'processing' | 'completed' | 'error';
  matchingError: string | null;
  extractedItemsCount: number;
  matchedItemsCount: number;
  
  // Step 5: Review
  reviewComplete: boolean;
}
```

**Example**:

```tsx
import { BOQWizardState } from "@/components/boq/BOQProcessingWizard";

// Use BOQWizardState in your code where appropriate.
```

#### `ColumnMapping`

- **Import**: `import { ColumnMapping } from "@/components/boq/BOQProcessingWizard";`
- **Kind**: Type

**Definition**:

```ts
export interface ColumnMapping {
  sheetName: string;
  itemCode: number | null;
  description: number | null;
  quantity: number | null;
  unit: number | null;
  supplyRate: number | null;
  installRate: number | null;
  totalRate: number | null;
  amount: number | null;
}
```

### `@/components/cable-route/utils/pathfinding`

- **Source**: `src/components/cable-route/utils/pathfinding.ts`

#### `PathFinder`

- **Import**: `import { PathFinder } from "@/components/cable-route/utils/pathfinding";`
- **Kind**: Class

**Definition**:

```ts
export class PathFinder {
  private width: number;
  private height: number;
  private gridSize: number;
  private obstacles: Obstacle[];

  constructor(
    width: number,
    height: number,
    obstacles: Obstacle[] = [],
    gridSize: number = 50
  ) {
    this.width = width;
    this.height = height;
    this.gridSize = gridSize;
    this.obstacles = obstacles;
  }

  private snapToGrid(point: Point3D): { x: number; y: number } {
    return {
      x: Math.round(point.x / this.gridSize) * this.gridSize,
      y: Math.round(point.y / this.gridSize) * this.gridSize,
    };
  }

  private isColliding(x: number, y: number): boolean {
    return this.obstacles.some(
      (obs) =>
        x >= obs.x &&
        x <= obs.x + obs.width &&
        y >= obs.y &&
        y <= obs.y + obs.height
    );
  }

  private heuristic(a: { x: number; y: number }, b: { x: number; y: number }): number {
    // Euclidean distance
    return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(b.x - a.x, 2) + Math.pow(b.y - a.y, 2));
  }

  private getNeighbors(node: GridNode): GridNode[] {
    const neighbors: GridNode[] = [];
    const directions = [
      { x: 0, y: -1 }, // North
      { x: 1, y: 0 },  // East
      { x: 0, y: 1 },  // South
      { x: -1, y: 0 }, // West
      { x: 1, y: -1 }, // NE (diagonal)
      { x: 1, y: 1 },  // SE
      { x: -1, y: 1 }, // SW
      { x: -1, y: -1 },// NW
    ];

    for (const dir of directions) {
      const newX = node.x + dir.x * this.gridSize;
      const newY = node.y + dir.y * this.gridSize;

      if (
        newX >= 0 &&
        newX <= this.width &&
        newY >= 0 &&
        newY <= this.height &&
        !this.isColliding(newX, newY)
      ) {
        // Penalty for diagonal moves to prefer orthogonal routes
        const isDiagonal = dir.x !== 0 && dir.y !== 0;
        const penalty = isDiagonal ? 1.4 : 1.0;

        neighbors.push({
          x: newX,
          y: newY,
          g: 0,
          h: 0,
          f: 0,
          parent: node,
        });
      }
    }

    return neighbors;
  }

  private reconstructPath(endNode: GridNode): Point3D[] {
    const path: Point3D[] = [];
    let current: GridNode | null = endNode;

    while (current) {
      path.unshift({ x: current.x, y: current.y, z: 0 });
      current = current.parent;
    }

    return this.simplifyPath(path);
  }

  private simplifyPath(path: Point3D[]): Point3D[] {
    if (path.length <= 2) return path;

    const simplified: Point3D[] = [path[0]];

    for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
      const prev = path[i - 1];
      const curr = path[i];
      const next = path[i + 1];

      // Check if points are collinear
      const dx1 = curr.x - prev.x;
      const dy1 = curr.y - prev.y;
      const dx2 = next.x - curr.x;
      const dy2 = next.y - curr.y;

      // If not collinear, keep the point
      if (dx1 * dy2 !== dy1 * dx2) {
        simplified.push(curr);
      }
    }

    simplified.push(path[path.length - 1]);
    return simplified;
  }

  findPath(start: Point3D, end: Point3D): Point3D[] {
    const snappedStart = this.snapToGrid(start);
    const snappedEnd = this.snapToGrid(end);

    const openSet: GridNode[] = [];
    const closedSet = new Set<string>();

    const startNode: GridNode = {
      x: snappedStart.x,
      y: snappedStart.y,
      g: 0,
      h: this.heuristic(snappedStart, snappedEnd),
      f: 0,
      parent: null,
    };
    startNode.f = startNode.g + startNode.h;

    openSet.push(startNode);

    while (openSet.length > 0) {
      // Find node with lowest f score
      openSet.sort((a, b) => a.f - b.f);
      const current = openSet.shift()!;

      // Check if we reached the goal
      if (current.x === snappedEnd.x && current.y === snappedEnd.y) {
        return this.reconstructPath(current);
      }

      closedSet.add(`${current.x},${current.y}`);

      for (const neighbor of this.getNeighbors(current)) {
        const key = `${neighbor.x},${neighbor.y}`;
        if (closedSet.has(key)) continue;

        const tentativeG = current.g + this.heuristic(current, neighbor);

        const existingNode = openSet.find((n) => n.x === neighbor.x && n.y === neighbor.y);

        if (!existingNode || tentativeG < existingNode.g) {
          neighbor.g = tentativeG;
          neighbor.h = this.heuristic(neighbor, snappedEnd);
          neighbor.f = neighbor.g + neighbor.h;
          neighbor.parent = current;

          if (!existingNode) {
            openSet.push(neighbor);
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // No path found, return direct line
    return [start, end];
  }
}
```

**Example**:

```tsx
import { PathFinder } from "@/components/cable-route/utils/pathfinding";

// Use PathFinder in your code where appropriate.
```

```ts
export interface CreateCircuitMaterialInput {
  circuit_id: string | null; // null for unassigned materials
  description: string;
  unit?: string;
  quantity?: number;
  supply_rate?: number;
  install_rate?: number;
  boq_item_code?: string;
  master_material_id?: string;
  final_account_item_id?: string;
  canvas_line_id?: string; // Link to canvas line for sync deletion
  // Optional overrides for auto-categorization
  material_category?: MaterialCategory;
  boq_section?: BOQSection;
  skip_supporting_materials?: boolean;
  // For unassigned materials - required when circuit_id is null
  project_id?: string;
  floor_plan_id?: string;
}
```

```ts
  cellClassName?: string;
}
```

### `@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useDebouncedCallback`

- **Source**: `src/components/floor-plan/hooks/useDebouncedCallback.ts`

#### `useDebouncedCallback`

- **Import**: `import { useDebouncedCallback } from "@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useDebouncedCallback";`
- **Kind**: Hook
- **Signature**: `useDebouncedCallback(callback: T, delay: number, leading?: boolean): T & { cancel: () => void; }`

Creates a debounced version of a callback that delays invoking until after
a specified delay has elapsed since the last time it was invoked.


**Example**:

```tsx
import { useDebouncedCallback } from "@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useDebouncedCallback";

export function Example() {
  const result = useDebouncedCallback();
  void result;
  return null;
}
```

### `@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useOptimisticUpdate`

#### `useOptimisticUpdate`

- **Import**: `import { useOptimisticUpdate } from "@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useOptimisticUpdate";`
- **Kind**: Hook
- **Signature**: `useOptimisticUpdate(initialValue: T, onCommit: (value: T) => void): { value: T; updateOptimistic: (updater: T | ((prev: T) => T)) => void; commit: () => void; commitImmediate: () => void; isPending: boolean; }`

Hook for managing optimistic UI updates during drag operations.
Provides immediate visual feedback while batching actual state updates.


**Example**:

```tsx
import { useOptimisticUpdate } from "@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useOptimisticUpdate";

export function Example() {
  const result = useOptimisticUpdate();
  void result;
  return null;
}
```

#### `useThrottledCallback`

- **Import**: `import { useThrottledCallback } from "@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useThrottledCallback";`
- **Kind**: Hook
- **Signature**: `useThrottledCallback(callback: T, limit: number): T`

Creates a throttled version of a callback that only invokes at most once
per specified time period.


**Example**:

```tsx
import { useThrottledCallback } from "@/components/floor-plan/hooks/useThrottledCallback";

  const result = useThrottledCallback();
  void result;
  return null;
}
```

#### `CircuitCable`

- **Import**: `import { CircuitCable } from "@/components/floor-plan/types";`
- **Kind**: Type

**Definition**:

```ts
export interface CircuitCable {
  id: string;
  points: Point[];
  measuredLength: number; // Auto-calculated from points using scale
  totalLength: number; // Measured + start/end heights
  // Circuit Details
  circuitRef?: string; // e.g., "L1", "P3"
  circuitType?: 'lighting' | 'power' | 'hvac' | 'data' | 'fire' | 'other';
  cableType?: string; // e.g., "4Core x 16mm Alu"
  from?: string; // Origin location
  to?: string; // Destination location
  // Routing Details
  containmentType?: string; // e.g., "Cable Tray", "Conduit"
  startHeight?: number; // Drop height at start (meters)
  endHeight?: number; // Drop height at end (meters)
  // BOQ Linking
  finalAccountItemId?: string; // Link to final_account_items
  boqItemCode?: string; // BOQ item reference
  // Costing
  supplyRate?: number;
  installRate?: number;
  totalCost?: number;
  // Meta
  notes?: string;
  color?: string; // Display color
}
```

**Example**:

```tsx
import { CircuitCable } from "@/components/floor-plan/types";

// Use CircuitCable in your code where appropriate.
```

### `@/components/floor-plan/utils`

- **Source**: `src/components/floor-plan/utils.ts`

#### `calculateLvCableSummary`

- **Import**: `import { calculateLvCableSummary } from "@/components/floor-plan/utils";`
- **Kind**: Function
- **Signature**: `calculateLvCableSummary(lines: SupplyLine[]): { totalLength: number; summary: Map<string, { totalLength: number; color: string; }>; terminationSummary: Map<string, number>; }`

Calculates the summary for LV cables, applying a multiplier for GP wires.


**Example**:

```tsx
import { calculateLvCableSummary } from "@/components/floor-plan/utils";

const result = calculateLvCableSummary(/* ...args */);
void result;
```

#### `getCableColor`

- **Import**: `import { getCableColor } from "@/components/floor-plan/utils";`
- **Kind**: Function
- **Signature**: `getCableColor(cableType: string): string`

Generates a consistent color for a given cable type string.
It uses a simple hashing algorithm to pick a color from the predefined
palette, ensuring the same string always returns the same color.


**Example**:

```tsx
import { getCableColor } from "@/components/floor-plan/utils";

const result = getCableColor(/* ...args */);
void result;
```

#### `getContainmentStyle`

#### `getCableColor`

- **Import**: `import { getCableColor } from "@/components/floor-plan/utils/styleUtils";`
- **Kind**: Function
- **Signature**: `getCableColor(cableType: string): string`

Generates a consistent color for a given cable type string.
It uses a simple hashing algorithm to pick a color from the predefined
palette, ensuring the same string always returns the same color.

#### `LightingLayerControls`

- **Import**: `import LightingLayerControls from "@/components/lighting/floorplan/LightingLayerControls";`
- **Kind**: Component
- **Signature**: `LightingLayerControls({ isVisible, onVisibilityChange, opacity, onOpacityChange, filterType, onFilterTypeChange, colorMode, onColorModeChange, onExportToSchedule, placementCount, totalWattage }: LightingLayerControlsProps): JSX.Element`

**Props**:
- **`colorMode`**: `"status" | "type"`
- **`filterType`**: `string`
- **`isVisible`**: `boolean`
- **`onColorModeChange`**: `(mode: "type" | "status") => void`
- **`onExportToSchedule`**: `() => void`
- **`onFilterTypeChange`**: `(type: string | null) => void`
- **`onOpacityChange`**: `(opacity: number) => void`
- **`onVisibilityChange`**: `(visible: boolean) => void`
- **`opacity`**: `number`
- **`placementCount`**: `number`
- **`totalWattage`**: `number`

**Example**:


```ts
export interface ExtractedLightingData {
  manufacturer: string | null;
  model_name: string | null;
  wattage: number | null;
  lumen_output: number | null;
  wattage_variants: WattageVariant[] | null;
  color_temperature: number | null;
  cri: number | null;
  beam_angle: number | null;
  ip_rating: string | null;
  ik_rating: string | null;
  dimensions: {
    length: number;
    width: number;
    height: number;
  } | null;
  weight: string | null;
  lifespan_hours: number | null;
  dimmable: boolean | null;
  driver_type: string | null;
}
```

### `@/components/master-library/development-phases/PhaseCard`

- **Source**: `src/components/master-library/development-phases/PhaseCard.tsx`

#### `PhaseCard`

- **Import**: `import { PhaseCard } from "@/components/master-library/development-phases/PhaseCard";`
- **Kind**: Component
- **Signature**: `PhaseCard({ phase, checkedItems, status, notes, onToggleItem, onSetStatus, onSetNotes, onReset, dependenciesMet, }: PhaseCardProps): JSX.Element`

**Props**:
- **`checkedItems`**: `string[]`
- **`dependenciesMet`**: `boolean`
- **`notes`**: `string`
- **`onReset`**: `() => void`
- **`onSetNotes`**: `(notes: string) => void`
- **`onSetStatus`**: `(status: PhaseStatus) => void`
- **`onToggleItem`**: `(itemId: string) => void`
- **`phase`**: `DevelopmentPhase`
- **`status`**: `PhaseStatus`

**Example**:


```ts
  page: number;
}
```

**Example**:

```tsx

// Use ExtractedImage in your code where appropriate.
```

#### `ExtractedShape`

- **Import**: `import { ExtractedShape } from "@/components/pdf-editor/PDFVisualExtractor";`
- **Kind**: Type

**Definition**:

```ts
export interface ExtractedShape {
  id: string;
  type: 'line' | 'rect' | 'path';
  x: number;
  y: number;
  width: number;
  height: number;
  strokeColor?: string;
  fillColor?: string;
  strokeWidth?: number;
  page: number;
  path?: string; // SVG path for complex shapes
}
```

**Example**:

```tsx
import { ExtractedShape } from "@/components/pdf-editor/PDFVisualExtractor";

// Use ExtractedShape in your code where appropriate.
```

- **`activeTool`**: `"select" | "pan" | "scale" | "zone"`
- **`existingScale`**: `number`
- **`isScaleMode`**: `boolean`
- **`isZoneMode`**: `boolean`
- **`onScaleLineComplete` (optional)**: `(start: Point, end: Point) => void`
- **`onScaleLineUpdate`**: `(line: { start: Point | null; end: Point | null; }) => void`
- **`onZoneComplete` (optional)**: `(points: Point[]) => void`
- **`onZonesChange`**: `(zones: Zone[]) => void`
- **`onZoneSelected` (optional)**: `(zoneId: string, tenantId: string | null) => void`
- **`pdfDoc`**: `PDFDocumentProxy`
- **`projectId`**: `string`
- **`scaleLine`**: `{ start: Point | null; end: Point | null; }`
- **`tenants`**: `any[]`
- **`zoneOpacity` (optional)**: `number`
- **`zones`**: `Zone[]`

**Example**:

```tsx
import { MaskingCanvas } from "@/components/tenant/MaskingCanvas";

export function Example() {
  return <MaskingCanvas activeTool={undefined as any} existingScale={0} isScaleMode={true} isZoneMode={true} onScaleLineUpdate={() => {}} onZonesChange={() => {}} pdfDoc={undefined as any} projectId="..." />;
}
```

```ts
  includeFloorPlan: boolean;
  contactId: string;

    showIcons: boolean;
    showBorders: boolean;
  };
  kpiCards: {

    totalArea: boolean;
    totalDbCost: boolean;
    totalLightingCost: boolean;

    shopNumber: boolean;

    layoutReceived: boolean;

    dbCost: boolean;
    lightingOrdered: boolean;
```
